                <tr id="so1" style="background-color: #FFF;"><td colspan="5" style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="width:100%; font-size:10pt"><center>Profiles:&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa9"  href="javascript:showMoreSO2017();">2017</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;(Click Year to Expand / <a href="javascript:hideSO('so1');">Close</a>)</center></div></td></tr>
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                <tr id="so9" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>You could be forgiven for thinking of Aaron Blair as an afterthought in 2015's Shelby Miller trade, given that the Braves also received Ender Inciarte and Dansby Swanson for their young pitcher. Blair was no throw-in, though; he pitched an excellent 2.92 ERA between AA and AAA for the Diamondbacks (albeit with a 4.01 FIP), and slotted in as a top-10 prospect in a crowded Braves farm system. Blair was quickly promoted to the majors in 2016, but got off to a rocky start, not showing the command he needed to succeed (10.5% BB% and only a 14.2% K%) and giving up a 7.99 ERA before being sent back down to the minors. Blair injured his knee and was removed from the rotation at one point, but did come back for a few solid starts at the season's end. Blair's underlying peripherals reveal no major red flags -- and he's only 24 -- so he's a good candidate to regress, and likely even improve on his underlying rates, in 2017. With Colon, Dickey and Jaime Garcia suiting up for the Braves this year, though, Blair's rotation slot isn't a given; even if it is, his upside is probably that of an average pitcher and a bench option in fantasy. (Brice Russ)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Blair came well-heralded from the Diamondbacks last year, but once he got to the majors, he lost his command and couldn't strike anyone out -- not a good combination. Blair is likely to improve next year, but isn't guaranteed a rotation slot and has league-average upside at best.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
            </table>
